<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">■</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">6.1 帳票管理マスタ</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>

<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>
<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>

<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>

<td style="background-color:#FDEDDA;color:#FDEDDA">&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>

<td >&nbsp;</td>

<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >現行システムの課題であった帳票ごとの個別管理によるメンテナンス負荷を解消し、</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >一括設定と個別設定の階層管理により、ユーザー自身での迅速かつ柔軟な運用変更を可能とする。</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
<td >&nbsp;</td>
